# Machine-learning
problem 1 
#importing
import sys, array, tempfile, heapq,random
import numpy as np

#generating the list of random integers

list1 = [random.randint(1,100) for _ in range(10000000)]



#sorting the list of random integers
heapq.heapify(list1)
new_list = []
while list1:
    new_list.append(heapq.heappop(list1))
#printing the sorted list    
print(new_list)

Problem 2

import pandas as pd
#read data from json file

data_df = pd.read_json('C:\\Users\\Mahasweta\\Downloads\\searches.json', lines=True)

df = pd.DataFrame(data_df)


a = df['uid']
b = []
#finding the odd and even uid
for i in a:  
    
    if (i % 2) == 0:
        b.append('E')       
         
    else: 
        b.append('O')
        
        
#appending the  dataframe with odd or even    
df['tp'] = b
#counting and grouping the datafame by even,odd and search_count   
h = df.groupby(['tp','search_count']).count()

#printing the dataframe with counting and grouping
print(h)
